/* =============================================================================                                                                                
Program     : I9_Formats.Txt                                                                                                                                    
Date Revised: 04/16/2015                                                                                                                                        
Descripiton :                                                                                                                                                   
Create SAS formats that may be used with SAS procedures to label the values of                                                                                  
ICD-9-CM Diagnoses and Procedures.  The values are updated through Version 32                                                                                   
of the ICD-9-CM codes and include both current and obsolete codes.  For example,                                                                                
the following SAS statements use the $I9DXF format with the Freq Procedure to                                                                                   
label the values of DX1 in the frequency listing:                                                                                                               
                                                                                                                                                                
    Proc Freq Data = NIS_2013_CORE ;                                                                                                                            
         Table DX1 ;                                                                                                                                            
         Format DX1 $I9DXF. ;                                                                                                                                   
    Run ;                                                                                                                                                       
                                                                                                                                                                
The following tables list formats available for selected HCUP data elements.                                                                                    
                                                                                                                                                                
    Core File                                                                                                                                                   
    Data Element(s)         Format Name(s)                                                                                                                      
    ===============         ==============                                                                                                                      
    ECODE1-ECODE4           $I9DXF. or $ECODE.                                                                                                                  
    DX1-DX25                $I9DXF. or $FDX.                                                                                                                    
    PR1-PR15                $I9PRF. or $FPR.                                                                                                                    
============================================================================= */                                                                                
                                                                                                                                                                
Proc Format ;                                                                                                                                                   
     Value $ECODE /* ECODEn - E code n */                                                                                                                       
           "E87  " - "E8799",                                                                                                                                   
           "E93  " - "E9399",                                                                                                                                   
           "E94  " - "E9499"    = "Medical misadventure/adverse reaction E code"                                                                                
           "E849 " - "E8499"    = "Place of occurrence"                                                                                                         
           "E8694",                                                                                                                                             
           "E967 " - "E9679"    = "Other type of E code"                                                                                                        
           "invl "              = "Invalid E code (invl)"                                                                                                       
           "incn "              = "Inconsistent E code (incn)"                                                                                                  
           "     "              = "Blank"                                                                                                                       
           OTHER                = "Injury E code"                                                                                                               
           ;                                                                                                                                                    
                                                                                                                                                                
     Value $FDX /* DXn - Diagnosis */                                                                                                                           
           " "    = "Blank"                                                                                                                                     
           "invl" = "Invalid DX (invl)"                                                                                                                         
           "incn" = "Inconsistent DX (incn)"                                                                                                                    
           OTHER  = "Valid DX"                                                                                                                                  
           ;                                                                                                                                                    
                                                                                                                                                                
     Value $FPR /* PRn - Procedure */                                                                                                                           
           "    " = "Blank"                                                                                                                                     
           "invl" = "Invalid PR (invl)"                                                                                                                         
           "incn" = "Inconsistent PR (incn)"                                                                                                                    
           OTHER  = "Valid PR"                                                                                                                                  
           ;                                                                                                                                                    
Value $I9DXF /* DX1-n */
   "     " = "     : BLANK"
